CREATE TABLE `dealerexcisedetails` (
    `id` VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    `RG23DEntryNumber` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT "",
    `supplierRG23DEntry` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT "",
    `assessableValue` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT "",
    `PLARG23DEntry` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT "",
    `manuAssessableValue` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT "",
    `goodsreceiptdetails` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
    `seqformat` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
    `seqnumber` INT(12) DEFAULT '0',
    `datesuffixvalue` VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT "",
    `datepreffixvalue` VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT "",
    `company` VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT "",
    `autogen` CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'F',
    PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
    CONSTRAINT FK_goodsreceipt_rg23d FOREIGN KEY (goodsreceiptdetails) REFERENCES grdetails(`id`)ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT  FK_rg23Dseqformat FOREIGN KEY (`seqformat`) REFERENCES `sequenceformat` (`id`),
    CONSTRAINT  FK_company_rg23Dseqformat FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;



CREATE TABLE `supplierexcisedetails` (
    `id` VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    `goodsreceiptdetailsId` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT "",
    `invoicedetails` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL,
    `vendor` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL,
    `natureofpurchase` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL,
    `utilizedQuantity` INT(50) DEFAULT 0,
    `actualQuantity` INT(50) DEFAULT 0,
    `company` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
    CONSTRAINT  FK_vendor_supplierDetails FOREIGN KEY (`vendor`) REFERENCES `vendor` (`id`),
    CONSTRAINT  FK_invoicedetails_supplierDetails FOREIGN KEY (`invoicedetails`) REFERENCES `invoicedetails` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT  FK_company_supplierDetails FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
    CONSTRAINT  FK_nop_supplierDetails FOREIGN KEY (`natureofpurchase`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

update default_header set islineitem = 'T',ismandatory='F',dataindex='taxid' where module='12' and defaultHeader = 'Tax';
update default_header set islineitem = 'T',ismandatory='T' where module='12' and defaultHeader = 'Reason';
update default_header set islineitem = 'T',ismandatory='F' where module='12' and defaultHeader = 'Description';

ALTER TABLE `creditnote` ADD COLUMN `masteragent`  varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 NULL DEFAULT NULL;
ALTER TABLE `creditnote` ADD FOREIGN KEY (`masteragent`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION;

ALTER TABLE `extracompanypreferences` ADD COLUMN `servicetaxadvpaymentacc` varchar(255) DEFAULT "";

 CREATE TABLE `defaultmobilefieldsetup` (
`id`  varchar(255) NOT NULL ,
`moduleid` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
`summaryreportjson`  LONGTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL ,
`detailreportjson`  LONGTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL,
`formfieldjson`  LONGTEXT  NULL DEFAULT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
KEY `fk_defaultmobilefieldsetup_moduleid` (`moduleid`))
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

    
CREATE TABLE `mobilefieldsetup` (
`id`  varchar(40) NOT NULL ,
`moduleid` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
`company` VARCHAR(40) DEFAULT NULL,
`summaryreportjson`  LONGTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL ,
`detailreportjson`  LONGTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL,
`formfieldjson`  LONGTEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
KEY `fk_mobilefieldsetup_company` (`company`),
KEY `fk_mobilefieldsetup_moduleid` (`moduleid`))
ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARACTER SET=utf8;

#Deepak Singh 16th August 2016

#To update Account in Credit Note table.
UPDATE creditnote cn
    SET account = (
        SELECT account
        FROM jedetail jed
        WHERE jed.id = cn.centry) where cn.isopeningbalencecn<>1;

#To update Account in Debit Note table.
UPDATE debitnote dn 
    SET account = (
        SELECT account
        FROM jedetail jed
        WHERE jed.id = dn.centry) where dn.isopeningbalencedn<>1;

#Ashish Mohite 26th August 2016
ALTER TABLE extracompanypreferences ADD COLUMN negativevaluein INT DEFAULT "2";

# Basaprabhu Ajur 2016-08-26
ALTER TABLE `in_stockmovement` ADD COLUMN `memo`  varchar(255) NULL DEFAULT NULL ;

UPDATE in_stockmovement sm 
INNER JOIN deliveryorder d ON d.id =sm.modulerefid 
INNER JOIN dodetails dtl ON dtl.deliveryorder=d.id AND sm.product=dtl.product
SET sm.memo=d.memo
WHERE sm.transactionno=d.donumber AND sm.transaction_module=6 AND sm.transaction_type=2 AND d.company=sm.company AND sm.product=dtl.product;

UPDATE in_stockmovement sm 
INNER JOIN salesreturn d ON d.id =sm.modulerefid 
INNER JOIN srdetails dtl ON dtl.salesreturn=d.id AND sm.product=dtl.product
SET sm.memo=d.memo
WHERE  sm.transactionno=d.srnumber AND sm.transaction_module=9 AND sm.transaction_type=1 AND sm.product=dtl.product AND d.company=sm.company;

UPDATE in_stockmovement sm 
INNER JOIN grorder d ON d.id =sm.modulerefid 
INNER JOIN grodetails dtl ON dtl.grorder=d.id AND sm.product=dtl.product
SET sm.memo=d.memo
WHERE  sm.transactionno=d.gronumber AND sm.transaction_module=5 AND sm.transaction_type=1 AND sm.product=dtl.product AND d.company=sm.company;

UPDATE  in_stockmovement sm 
INNER JOIN in_stockadjustment d ON d.id =sm.modulerefid 
INNER JOIN in_sa_detail dtl ON dtl.stockadjustment=d.id AND sm.product=d.product
set sm.memo=d.memo
WHERE  sm.transactionno=d.seqno AND sm.transaction_module=3 AND sm.transaction_type=2 AND sm.product=d.product AND d.company=sm.company;
